En los dispositivos híbridos y las tabletas como Microsoft Surface, ni siquiera tendrá que reiniciar la aplicación.\r\n\r\n Grapholite se puede usar para:\r\n\r\n•         diagramas de flujo;\r\n•         diagramas de canales Swimlanes;\r\n•         organigramas;\r\n•         diagramas UMLs;\r\n•         estructuras de sitios web y wireframes;\r\n•         croquis de interfaces de aplicaciones (maquetas UI);\r\n•         distribuciones de redes (incluidas las redes Cisco);\r\n•         planos (de oficina, plantas de edificios, viviendas, etc.);\r\n•         modelos de negocio (se admiten tanto BPMN 1.2 como BPMN 2.0);\r\n•         mapas conceptuales;\r\n•         diagramas de Venn y de otros tipos predefinidos;\r\n•         diagramas de flujo de datos;\r\n•         diagramas de flujo de procesos;\r\n•         flujo de trabajo;\r\n•         diagramas circulares incluidos los diagramas Chevron;\r\n•         análisis DAFO;\r\n•         ilustraciones científicas;\r\n•         gráficos, algoritmos, esquemas;\r\n•         planogramas;\r\n•         infografías.\r\n\r\nLa aplicación proporciona un conjunto único de comportamientos de formas para cada tipo de diagrama. Por ejemplo, las ventanas y las puertas se conectan automáticamente a las paredes en los planos de planta; las formas admiten el diseño automático de los elementos secundarios y la reducción o la expansión de los niveles de jerarquía en organigramas y mapas  conceptuales. La lógica de enrutamiento automático de las conexiones también depende del tipo de diagrama.\r\n\r\nEl panel de objetos permite ver, seleccionar, bloquear y ocultar todos los objetos visuales.\r\nImprima, comparta o exporte sus diagramas e insértelos en sus sitios web, publicaciones de blog, artículos, documentos, hojas de cálculo, presentaciones  y otros medios.\r\n\r\nGrapholite puede exportar datos en formatos Pdf, Png, Jpeg, Svg y Microsoft Visio (Vdx). También se pueden importar archivos de Microsoft Visio tanto en los formatos Vdx como Vsdx (Visio 2013). \r\n\r\nLa aplicación es compatible con iPad, Desktop, Windows Phone y Android.\r\n\r\nLa is a brand-new title from the creators of This War of Mine. It’s a society survival game that asks what people are capable of when pushed to the brink of extinction. In an entirely frozen world, people develop steam-powered technology to oppose the overwhelming cold. The city’s ruler has to manage both the citizens and the infrastructure they live in. The leader’s tactical skills face challenges that will frequently question morality and the basic foundations of what we consider organized society. Optimization and resource management often clash with empathy and thoughtful decision-making. While city and society management will consume most of the ruler’s time, at some point exploration of the outside world is necessary to understand its history and present state.\r\n\r\nWhat decisions will you make to ensure the survival of your society? What will you do when pushed to the limit? And...\r\n\r\n...who will you become in the process?\r\n\r\nMAKE THE LAW\r\nSociety is a group of people who abide by the same rules and share similar beliefs. Establish laws that regulate the existence of your growing society. Decide on their working routine, healthcare, food provision and other crucial aspects of everyday life. Maintain their hope and contentment – the moral condition of your society is as important as securing the basic means to keep them fed and safe.\r\n\r\nWEIGH UP YOUR CHOICES\r\nSome of your decisions will seem small – like deciding the fate of a troubled citizen or meeting the demands of a newborn faction – but be aware that the sum of your doings can lead to unexpected results. Your people put their faith in you, but their devotion is not limitless. Leadership can be a burden.\r\n\r\nDEVELOP NEW TECHNOLOGIES\r\nSurvival demands progress. React to current events, but don’t forget about the long term and investing in development and technological progress. Providing a highly advanced infrastructure with self-powered automatons, airships and other technical wonders is difficult, but achievable. It all depends on your management and leadership skills.\r\n\r\nEXPLORE THE FROSTLAND\r\nWhile New London is your main focus, there is much more to the world than what lies within the limits of your city. Expeditions, while risky, can bring you valuable intel, precious supplies and grow your society’s population. There may be people out there, and their fate lies solely in your hands.\r\n\r\nSHAPE YOUR SOCIETY\r\nIf you reach a turning point, do not hesitate to determine the path of your people.
